[38;2;255;255;255m⏺[39m [1mRoot Cause Analysis[22m

  [1mTASK_COMPLETE[22m

  The program crashes due to a [1mnull pointer dereference[22m in the [38;2;177;185;249madd_score[39m
  function at line 26 of [38;2;177;185;249mdemo-buggy.c[39m.

  [1mRoot Cause:[22m
  - The [38;2;177;185;249mcreate_student[39m function (lines 12-20) intentionally sets [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores [39m
  = NULL instead of allocating memory for the scores array
  - When [38;2;177;185;249madd_score[39m is called, it attempts to write to
  [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[s->num_scores][39m which is effectively writing to address 0x0
  - This causes a segmentation fault (EXC_BAD_ACCESS)

  [1mCrash Details:[22m
  - [1mLocation:[22m [38;2;177;185;249mdemo-buggy.c:26[39m in function [38;2;177;185;249madd_score[39m
  - [1mInstruction:[22m [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[s->num_scores] = score;[39m
  - [1mMemory Address:[22m 0x0 (NULL pointer)
  - [1mStudent State:[22m name="Alice", age=20, scores=0x0, num_scores=0

  [1mCall Stack:[22m
  1. [38;2;177;185;249mmain[39m calls [38;2;177;185;249madd_score(alice, 95.5)[39m at line 56
  2. [38;2;177;185;249madd_score[39m attempts to dereference NULL pointer at line 26
  3. CPU raises EXC_BAD_ACCESS exception

  The bug was intentionally introduced by commenting out the memory
  allocation for the scores array and explicitly setting it to NULL.
